Does not honor Yelp Check-in Discount and charges $60 if you enter after 8pm. Overall, they are ok. I liked the 4am access hour. I didn't like how they advertise access 4am-945pm, but conveniently leave out the  $60 charge if you want to access your items after 8pm. I also didn't like that they didn't honor the Yelp check-in discount of 50% for first 2 months. The lady was like, we don't have that discount. We can give you 20%. That's a dramatic difference and when I called to make my appt before I showed up with my belongings, I mentioned the discount. So that was frustrating. The lady finally was like, well I can give you 20% off of the first 3 months. Then I also mentioned that I have USAA rental insurance, so I don't have to pay the monthly  $9 fee. My phone was at literally 0% on power save mode, so I couldn't pull up the proof. I asked to use the store phone and was denied. (The lady said that they only have 1 line...) Then I was like well I will use my phone until it dies. She was like, " Well you only have 3minutes  to call USAA because the screen will timeout and you will have to go outside and use the kiosk because she has to go on lunch...... Which I believe several thungs she said was false. It was 1:30pm, so they would close the store at 1pm for lunch while other people are there? I honestly think she was bothered that I had a coupon and wanted to make my process as difficult as possible for me. The 2 reasons I choose this place over other locations was due to their hours and Yelp Check-in Discount, both which didn't workout how I thought!!</review>

< text>
Ok to be fair, this is of course a fast food restaurant. However, in all the fast food restaurants, this one is really our favorite!

Often we are so tired from work and just looking to have a quick dinner. Noodles & Company is always reliable, and with the free delivery from DoorDash it‚Äôs just the place for that last minute delicious lifesaver.

For those who‚Äôve never been there, Noodles & Company has a very simple menu. Few noodle choices served with different sauces like pesto, Alfredo, marinara... But the thing that appealing is that all their menu items can be made vegetarian! All of them!

I would highly recommend you‚Äôre try the Pesto Caviapatti. And the spaghetti Alfredo is one my favorites. Also FYI: their Mac-and-cheese side and tomato bisque soups are fantastic! Totally worth the extra $3.</text>

<Rating>1<//Rating>< review>
We first went the the Vancouver, WA location and we were thothoroughly impressed. Then this one opened up in our area. We have been probably 4 or 5 times and i just kept hoping it was "a bad batch" but no this location cant make decent pasta. I dont plan on ever going back. The butter noodles are LITTERALLY swiming in butter. There is almost more butter then noodle gross. And the mac n cheese was DISGUSTING. Mac n cheese is one of my 4 year olds FAVORITE and even she wouldnt eat it. Her mac n cheese litterally was a pile if noodles also swimming in greese with a TINY bit of cheese sprinkled on top. Flavor and quality aside  why anyone would pay that much money for 15 noodles is beyond me.

We ordered the butter noodles and mac n cheese at thr Vancouver location. The bowl of butter noodles was huge. Less greesy and more flavor. The mac n cheese was thick with cheese sauce.</review>

< Text>
Quiet, tucked away, and hiding some of the best surf on the central coast. There's a secret way to drive here but most people park along the highway and walk to the shore. You can also bike from Wilder Ranch in just a few minutes and enjoy the fantastic cliffside views. This area is also a legal drone flying area so you may hear some buzzing.<//Text>

< user_id>
115161532261487958597<//user_id>
<gmapID>0x808e425aead549d3:0xf74d7a067ae37bfb<//gmapID>< review>
It's been about a decade since the last time I've visited this beach. my older brother had brought our family here on an outing.. and I remember loving how quiet and chill this beach was (even though we found a huge dead seal that day)...
I was pleasantly surprised that it has not changed at all... you have to walk a bit of a distance to actually get to the beach/ocean, and it can get very windy, so I don't believe it would be a good idea to carry a whole bunch of stuff (like when you go to the boardwalk). It is a beautiful beach to go relax in with a blanket.. or walk along to the other side and look at the all the little shellfish that are growing on the rocks.. be super careful though, because the waves hit out of no where and can knock you down or into the ocean (if you do bring small kids, maybe don't go to that side of the beach)
I honestly think this beach is where people come out to go surfing though.. because I remember most of the people there were surfers back on my first visit here.. and the handful of people here today also all went out into the water.<//review>

< text>
This is one of our favorite beaches  We have been coming here for the last 10 years and the cleanliness at the beach has gone down. I think the literacy ( common sense index) rate has fallen down with people visiting. There is a big board which mentions "no dogs" allowed where as the beach has people coming with their dogs. As it is a no dog beach there is no requirement to cleanup after your dog is done with their waste management. The area around the beach has started smelling like one. "No fire or barbecue" allowed on the be beach which again is violated by the young crowd visiting the beach. Rangers should visit the beach more often to keep check on such violations so visitors to the beach can enjoy it more as it was before a few years back.</text>

<Text>You are paying for an experience. Please do not get this gem confused with a commercial style bar. I absolutely love speakeasies. So first it has a secret door and everything, my first thought was THIS IS THE REAL DEAL. You will step into be 20s and wish to never leave. The decor is gorgeous and the music is mood setting. When you sit you will be  blessed to encounter Tristan!!! He is nothing less than perfection. He is beyond knowledgeable and does it so effortlessly without making you feel inept. I mean the man has got to be the most well informed bartender ever. He is not one of these guys throwing your drinks together and moving on to the next patron. EVERYONE is hanging onto his every word craving the stories behind each drink he is crafting. He is not your average bartender ppl and you will not be paying an average price. This place is pricey and for good reason. 13 dollars a drink sounds crazy until you actually walk in and see what you are getting. I'm a penny pincher and would save just to have this experience. You have to try this place out. Don't miss out. Once you come here you'll never see bars the same. It was like I was living the  prohibition experience. Must try drinks Dead man's chest ($18) Wild wood, and a classic Whiskey sour. Not that out of the bottle foolishness. This is my new go to for drinks. It really changed my entire drinking experience.<//Text>< pics>

<userid>105957557158555793718<//userid><username>shawna</username><time>1556416532198< /time><rating>5< /rating>< Text>
This gem is tucked away in Devilicous at the end of Old Town Temecula and you will not only be wowed by the quality of the drinks but the atmosphere makes it a place you must visit at least once. It's got a very cool speakeasy vibe and decor that really gives the place a unique atmosphere. We ordered The Old Man and The Sea ($14) which has a black sea salt on the rim and contains egg white. It's got a salty but sweet taste, not too bitter. The texture of the egg white is what makes it. Second drink, served in a fresh coconut is The Dead Man's Chest ($18) which is similar to a Mai Tai. They serve it with a dried pineapple ringlet, which completes the sweet and tropical taste of this drink. We have been here a couple times and it's best to get there early or make a reservation as it does fill up quickly on the weekends. We will be back soon!< /Text>

As I walked into the restaurant I made obvious eye contact with the cashier directly behind the register. I smiled and approached to order, to which she immediately ran back into the kitchen as if I was invisible or just plain hideous. I waited patiently at the register until she finally came back. I greeted her with a happy smile. Before I could even open my mouth and say what I would like to order, she said that the ovens were off and that they only had 2 slices of pizza left. She said this with such a quickness I was shocked and confused. I didn't have time to process this at first. I am not sure what she thought I was in the store for with my group of friends, of course 2 slices was just a bit small for us. The most insulting part of this was that it was only 7:20pm and that they wouldn't be closing till 8pm. Why are the ovens off close to an hour before they close? They were trying to close early. We were all young once and yes it's great to have fun, but please update your hours that ovens close at 7pm so that this doesn't happen to another unfortunate soul. I just wanted some food after a hard day. It was my turn to treat my coworkers, who are also my best friends. They seemed like they were okay with it, but I felt terrible. I know eventually I'll get over this, but it just sucks. I had money in hand and ready to pay. It was a waste of time. <Text>TORTAS!!! Nom, nom, nom!

The Torta's here are huge! Apart from the generous portions all the ingredients tasted fresh. The tomatoes, avocados and even the bread. So far I tried the Milanesa, Cubana, Azada and the Hawaiana. I am delighted  to report that none of them were disappointing!

Then, there are the rest of the goodies in the store. The lines can get quite long, but they move along fairly quickly. I also ended up getting a Custard Horn, Mango Flan and a ChocoFlan cake.....YUM! None of the desserts were overly sweet. They were just so very well balanced and the chocolate tasted like it was genuine Coca, or maybe a decent bittersweet dark chocolate. I just wish this place had more seating and was in a slightly better location. It can be a bit challenging to order, I got the impression that the entire staff speaks broken English or very little English. The selection of baked goods here is immense, can't wait to try all of them!<//Text>< Pics>

<Review>The Food
When a friend sends you a picture of a giant sandwich and says "I would like a review". You bet I'll go and get the giant sandwich and do a review. I didn't know Mexico Bakery was a place until that day, and definitely did not know there's a giant sandwich. The giant sandwich refers to torta, which in this context is a sandwich. I order their combinada (combination) with 2 carnes (2 meats) with asada (beef) and cubana (cuban). But there's more, it comes with meat chili (sloppy joe?), egg, avocado, and an array of vegetables. When I say the sandwich was big, I mean it was as big as my face. I can't even fit it into my mouth. Even though it is like $16, it was not a bad deal. The only gripe I have was that the beef was dry and tough to chew, otherwise it was pretty good. The bakery has a variety of other selections, from pastries to desserts. Would like to return to check out their other items.

The Miscellaneous
The bakery is in a quite spacious plaza, with plenty of parking. The inside itself is not super big, but still decent sized. There seemed to be a small amount of seating before, but of course now is all take out. They have a straightforward menu you can order from, but many of the selection on display is not on the menu itself. The combine selection from the menu and display is quite extensive with many items. The prices are not bad, pretty reasonable.< /Review><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNrKF023BvMLEFS4MF8Nru7Y2ngZnPcS8EzKqZZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNT_ij2_a_F6_Wy0t6yD9XaM0zjUh7Ige1D4t1b=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pics><response>None<//response><gmap_id>0x808fcd448e1531ff:0x11108a1ef781c47f<//gmap_id></record>

<Rating>4</Rating><Text>I have been going to both this location and the other location (Santa Clara Street) for many years. Although this place is a bakery, it's well known for having excellent tortas. When I go, I usually either get a glazed donut or a churro to accompany my main dish. Now, if you fancy tortas, this is definitely the place to go. One, they are reasonably priced. Two, they give you a great amount of meat. <UserId.>105205158549678971888< /UserId.><Text>Really the only thing I have to say, they're the best. Killer tortas, they're so big I can't finish one. What's left over I can make another one later.< /Text><Pics>None<//Pics><user_name>Melody Boles</user_name></record></dataset><record>

< name>
Ahmad Jetha< /name>
<Time>1539539577794</Time><Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
Mexico Bakery popped up as the first result when searching for Mexican Bakeries in San Jose on Yelp. I decided to give it a try as it had a near perfect rating from almost 900 reviews. It is located in the eastern edge of the city so its not in the best part of town, but the location is not as sketchy as some of the other areas on the east side. There is a small parking lot in the front so parking is not an issue. At the peak lunch hour on a Saturday the place seemed pretty full with a line 5 people deep in front of the ordering station which is too your left when you enter. The baked goods and cakes are in the long display to your right. I did not see any anyone behind these displays so I skipped these items and got in line. I decided to get the Torta Milanesa ($8.50) which is fried breaded beef steak, to-go with everything. The lady behind the cash register spoke decent English so I did not face any issues during ordering.

After ordering I had to wait for around 15 minutes before I got my order. Here you get an order number but unfortunately the numbers are called out in Spanish so like me if you can‚Äôt speak Spanish it is a bit of a hassle. The good news is that orders are processed in order that they are received so if you track the person in front of you, you would know when you are up. It would be a lot easier if they simply called out numbers in Spanish and English, but that is too much to ask here.

I got a huge and I mean huge torta which had almost 3 layers of milanesa. This had to be the largest torta that I‚Äôd had in my life. The one word to describe it would be terrific. The only negative that I can think of is that it was a little heavy on the salt and it had a little too much Avocado for my taste so next time I‚Äôll skip the Avocado. Price wise it was slightly more than what you would pay for a burger in Five Guys so I‚Äôd say that it was in line with what you would pay for a comparable item in the area. Looking at the overall package or service, quality and value for money, Mexico Bakery definitely has me down as a fan. Hopefully I will figure out how to order the baked goods and try some of those and update my review at that time.</Review>

< Review>
Where do I begin?!! I love the tortas, especially the cubana. The sandwiches are made to order. Huge!! Fully loaded. Normally I would split with someone for a torta that size, but I always almost finish it myself, and save the rest for later.. They do not skimp on the avocado either like other places do.
Pastries: I have tried almost every thing and have loved it all. I do however recommend the chocoflan. So yum!
Service: there's one line for everything. But they are pretty quick in trying to help everyone. If the line starts to form, the workers in the back comes out to help out.</Review>

<text>I hear a rumbling in my tummy! Uh oh....where should I go?

I chose Bakery Mexico! I was sold on the "less than $5" meal since I was rolling on a budget to save for future trips and shopping expenses.

Among all the helpful tips from friends, you have two choices between their famous tortas: Milanesa or Cubano. Well, my SO and I ordered both to share each other's half and try what the other sandwich was like. My-oh-my!! I love both! I can't pinpoint any favoritism to which I enjoyed more. I found that both had incredible amount of meat, packed with avocado, tomato, eggs, hot dogs, etc. The juicy meat with all the dripping oil sliding down my hand, I almost had a heart attack! Their tortas was to die for! I couldn't finish the rest of mine, so I took it home to eat for later.

I'm not sure what else is there to say, other than, come here for their tortas! You won't be disappointed. The size of my two hands combined was the size of their tortas. Very filling and greasy but worth it! They also have pastry goodies, but I haven't had the chance to try any of it. I might come back for their slices of cake or cookies, because they priced it dirt cheap too!

Not bad. Not bad at all. I'm coming back!<//text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Response>
